 Kalpana Thodam, who reached the Bronze medal through repechage, won the Silver Medal by defeating Christiane Lagentill of Mauritius in the women's 52kg category
 unhone kam penlti ank (shido) hasil karte hue jeet darj kii
 Kalpana got two while Christian got three penalty points
 manajit nandal (purush 66 kigra) ko haalanki bronj medal ke mukaable main dakshin africa ke siabulila mabulu ke haathon shikast kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 Manjeet got three while Mabulu got two penalty points
 manajit or kalpana donon quarter final main haar gaye the, lekin donon ne rapeches main jeet darj karke bronj medal ke mukaable ke liye kwalifai kiya
 On the other hand, India had a good start in hockey, table tennis, badminton and squash, but swimmers and cyclists failed to make a significant impact
 badminton main bharat ne mishrit team spardhaa ke group bi match main ghana ko 5-0 se karaari shikast di
 India did not have to work hard to register this victory
 paroopalli kashyap ne danniel sam ko purush ekal mukaable main 21-6, 21-16 se shikast di
 World Championship bronze medalist PV Sindhu defeated Stella Amasa 21-7, 21-5
 purush yugal varg main akshay devalkar or pranav chopra ne emanual donkor or abraham e ko 21-7, 21-11 se maat di
 Commonwealth Games gold medalist duo Jwala Gutta and Ashwini Ponnappa defeated Evelyn Botwe and Diana Archer
 vahiin mishrit yugal main pisi tulsi or kidambi shrikant ne sam or amasah ko 21-5, 21-9 se haraaya
 In Table Tennis, India's men's and women's table tennis started off brilliantly and defeated Vanatu and Barbados respectively
 chaar saal pehle dilli kaamanwealth games main silver medal jeetne vaali mahila team ne shaamini kumarasen, manika batra or madhurika patkar ke shandaar pradarshan se barbados ko 3-0 se haraaya
 India's top player Sharath Kamal was rested in the men's opening match
 harmit desai, sanil shetty or anthony amalraj kii team ne bharat ko 3-0 se jeet dilaai
 In squash, Anaka Alankamony, Harinder Pal Sandhu and Mahesh Mangaonkar started with a win
 alankamoni ne round 32 main kenya kii khalka nimaji ko 11-2, 11-3, 11-6 se haraaya
 His next match will be against Malaysia's 15th seed Delia Arnold
 bharat kii chotii kii khilaadi deepika pallical or anbhavi joshna chinappa ko pehle daur main bai mili he
 In men's singles, Mangaonkar easily defeated Hardeep Riel of Kenya in round 64
 unhen ab england ke tisare variya peter barker kii kadi chunauti kaa saamana karnaa he
 Sandhu also made a good start by defeating Michael Craig of Northern Ireland 11-9, 11-5, 11-5
 bhartiya tairaak sajaan prakaash purushon kii 400 meter freestil tairaaki ke final main jagah banane main naakaam rahe
 Prakash scored three minutes 59 in heat number two
 29 second kaa samay nikaala or vah 28 tairaakon ke bich 20wein sthaan par rahe
 In the men's 100m freestyle S-9, Indian Para swimmer Prashant Karmakar scored a minute 4
 86 second kaa samay nikaalkar final main jagah banaai
 Karmakar, who won the Bronze medal at the Delhi Commonwealth Games, finished fourth in his heat
 cycling main bharatiyon kii shuruyaat acchhee nahin rahi
 Indian cyclists failed to qualify for the final of the men's sprint and the 4000-meter team Parasuite
 bhartiya mahila hockey team ne haalanki jeet se shuruyaat karte hue jasprit cor ke do gol kii madad se group e main canada ko 4-2 se haraaya
 India dominated the match from the very beginning and did not give Canada a chance to progress until the last
 bharat kii taraf se rani rampal (22wein minute), punam rani (30wein), jasprit (38 or 54wein minute) ne gol daage jabaki canada ke liye breani stayers or karli johansan ne gol kiye

 " The Dalai Lama, the spiritual guru of Buddhism in Tibet, has said that he may have an avatar in India after his death, where he has spent 60 years of his exile
 dalai lamas ne yah ashanka bhi jataai he ki unke maranoparant do dalai lamas ho sakate hai, jinamein se ek swatantra desh (bharat) se hoga jabaki doosraa china dwaara chunaa gaya hoga
 The Lai Lama has warned that no other heir named by China will be respected
 vahiin jaankaron kaa maananaa he ki china kii taraf se aglaa dalai lamas ghoshit hone kii vajah se bharat ke liye badi asahaj sthiti paidaa ho sakati he jo nehru yug se bhi buree ho sakati he
 China has rejected the Dalai Lama's declaration that a person named by China will not be respected, saying that the re-incarnation is a centuries-old practice in Tibetan Buddhism
 iskaa ek nishchit anushthan or parampara he
 Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesman Geng Shuang says that we respect and preserve these methods of Tibetan Buddhism
 saikadon saal se pun: avatar kii parampara he
 The 14th Dalai was also recognized by religious customs and was recognized by the Chinese government
 lihaaja dalai lamas ke punaravataar ko rashtriya niyam-kaayade or dharmik reeti-rivaaj kaa anusaran karnaa chahie
 The Chinese government has a policy of freedom of religious belief
 dalai lamas ne news agency royatres se baatcheet main kaha he ki china dalai lamas ke punarjanm ko bahut mahatvapurn maanata he
 He is more worried about the next Dalai Lama than me
 bhavishya main, yadi aap dekhte hai ki do dalai lamas aate hai, ek yahaan se, mukt desh main, ek chini dwaara chunaa jaataa he, to koi bhi bharosa nahin karegaa, koi bhi sammaan nahin karegaa (china dwaara chune gaye dalai lamas kaa)
 So this is a different problem for Chinese! Possible, it can happen
 jawahar laal nehru uniwarsity main centre for east-asian studies kii professor alka acharya kaa kahana he ki tibet ko china apana maanata he
 Tibetan Buddhism considers its internal matter
 agar dalai lamas chale gaye or jate-jate apane avatar ke bharat main hone kii ghoshnaa kar gaye, to china unke dwaara ghoshit agle dalai ko sweekaar nahin karegaa
 What would India do in such a situation? Professor Alka Acharya says that this situation will be worse for India than Nehru era
 kyonki china 14wein dalai lamas ko kitna bhi bhala-bura kahe lekin yah to maanata hi he ki vahi dalai hai

 china main buddha dharm ko maanane waalon kii badi aabaadi rahati he

 Let us tell that in 1950 China took Tibet under its control and he considers 14th Dalai Lama as separatist
 baharhaal 14wein dalai lamas ke bare main china kitna bhi bhala-bura kahe lekin tibeti buddha dharmaguru ke taur par unki manyata ko sweekaar to karata hi he
 But after the demise of the 83-year-old Dalai Lama, China may once again try to control the incarnation of the Dalai Lama, a symbol of Buddhist faith, given its strategic advantages
 jisaki ashanka khud dalai lamas ne jataai he
 In such a situation, India will be faced with a dilemma whether to accept the avatar announced by the Dalai Lama or the Dalai Lama declared by China

 tippaniyan In the KYC form, the consumer has to provide all the necessary information such as name, date of birth, father's name, mother's name, husband's or wife's name, address along with PIN code, and alternatively bank information
